 It was Tatya Tope who played an important role in the first fight for independence
 tope kaa naam un logon main shaamil he, jinhone sabase pehle angrejon ke khilaaf vidroh shuru kiya tha
 Let us know the important things related to his life and how he started the revolution of 1857
 
 
 - tathya tope kaa janm 1814 main ek marathi parivaar main hua tha
 His real name was Ramachandra Pandurang Rao, though people called him after Tatya Tope
 165 saal pehle aaj hi ke din bharat main chali thi pehali train- angrejon ke khilaaf hui 1857 kii kranti main tathya tope kaa bhi bada yogadan rahaa

 isi ke saath hi unhone angrejon ke khilaaf kai baar loha liya tha

 - kanpur main angrejon ko parajeet karne ke baad tathya ne jhaansi kii rani lakshmibai ke saath milakar madhya bharat kaa morcha sambhala tha

 haalanki unhen kai baar haar kaa saamana bhi karnaa padaa
 They were known to attack in their guerrilla ways

 - bharat ke kai hisson main unhone angrejon ke naak main dam kar diya or khaas baat ye thi ki angreji sena unhen pakadaney main naakaam rahi thi

 haalanki 8 april 1959 ko wo angrejon kii pakad main aa gaye or 15 april, 1959 ko shivpuri main tathya kaa court marshall kiya gaya

 - haalanki unki faansee par bhi kai sawaal uthaae gaye hai

 On 1 January 1859, Tatya Tope was martyred
